+struct ConVarFlags
+ConVarFlags s_flaggedConVars[] =
+	for ( int i=0; i<ARRAYSIZE( s_flaggedConVars ); ++i )
+		ConVar *flaggedConVar = cvar->FindVar( s_flaggedConVars[i].name );
+		if ( flaggedConVar )
+			flaggedConVar->AddFlags( s_flaggedConVars[i].flags );
+			if ( s_flaggedConVars[i].optional_default )
+				flaggedConVar->SetDefault( s_flaggedConVars[i].optional_default );
+				flaggedConVar->Revert();

+		ConVarRef var( pConVar );
+			ConVar *pConVar = (ConVar *)cvar->FindVar( m_ModifiedConvars[i].pszConvar );
+			if ( pConVar )
+				pConVar->SetValue( m_ModifiedConvars[i].pszOrgValue );
+			ConVar *pConVar = (ConVar *)cvar->FindVar( m_ModifiedConvars[i].pszConvar );
+			if ( pConVar )
+				pConVar->SetValue( m_ModifiedConvars[i].pszCurrentValue );

+	if (!pCommand && !pConVar)
+	if (pConVar && args.ArgC() == 3)
+		float currentValue = pConVar->GetFloat();
+	ConVar* pConVar = cvar->FindVar(cvarName);

+	bool requiresCheatFlag = pConVar->IsFlagSet(FCVAR_CHEAT);

+		pConVar->Revert();
+		if (Q_stricmp(pConVar->GetString(), newValue) == 0)
+		pConVar->SetValue(newValue);

+void ConVarRef::Init( const char *pName, bool bIgnoreMissing )
+	m_pConVar = g_pCVar ? g_pCVar->FindVar( pName ) : &s_EmptyConVar;
+	if ( !m_pConVar )
+		m_pConVar = &s_EmptyConVar;
+	m_pConVarState = static_cast< ConVar * >( m_pConVar );
+				Warning( "ConVarRef %s doesn't point to an existing ConVar\n", pName );
+ConVarRef::ConVarRef( IConVar *pConVar )
+	m_pConVar = pConVar ? pConVar : &s_EmptyConVar;
+	m_pConVarState = static_cast< ConVar * >( m_pConVar );
+bool ConVarRef::IsValid() const
+	return m_pConVar != &s_EmptyConVar;
